<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:quarantaine.html>quarantaine</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">quarantena</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">quadrāgintā</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:quarantaine.html>quarantaine</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:quarantaines.html>quarantaines</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:quarantaine.html>quarantainetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A quarantine, sanitary measure of isolating infected people; its duration or site</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Any isolation, exclusion</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:quarters.html>quarters</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">plural only<span class="ib-comma">,</span> military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Housing, barracks or other habitation or living space. Compare cuarto.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1913</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robert_Barr_(writer)" class="extiw" title="w:Robert Barr (writer)">Robert Barr</a>,  chapter 1, in  <cite>Lord Stranleigh Abroad</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://openlibrary.org/works/OL1796924W">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">“I have visited my <b><a href = vnd.unilang:quarters.html>quarters</a></b>, and find them very comfortable.<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span>Steerage <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> like everything else maritime<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span>vastly improved since Robert <a href = vnd.unilang:louis.html>Louis</a> Stevenson <a href = vnd.unilang:took.html>took</a> his trip third class to New York.”</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The place where someone or something <a href = vnd.unilang:lives.html>lives</a>
<ul><li><b>2017,</b> Jennifer S. Holland, <i>For These <a href = vnd.unilang:monkeys.html>Monkeys</a>, It’s a Fight for Survival.</i>, National Geographic (March 2017)<a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.nationalgeographic.com/magazine/2017/03/macaques-monkeys-indonesia-endangered-pet-trade/">[2]</a>
<dl><dd>The local pet trade thrives on captured or orphaned <a href = vnd.unilang:baby.html>baby</a> macaques—often malnourished and kept in tight <b><a href = vnd.unilang:quarters.html>quarters</a></b>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A commonly played university drinking game in North America.</li>
<li>Quarterfinals.</li></ol>

***quiche.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:quiche.html>quiche</a> (26064)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <a href = vnd.unilang:lorraine.html>Lorraine</a> <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rhenish_Franconian_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Rhenish Franconian languages">Rhine Franconian</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmw-rfr">Küeche</i>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">kuoche</i>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">kuocho</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">kuohho</i>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kōkô</i>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gog</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ball-shaped object</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. First attested in French in 1805. More at <span class="Latn" lang="en">cake</span>.
</p>

***quicksilver.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:quicksilver.html>quicksilver</a> (80195)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">quyk silver</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">quyksilver</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">quikselver</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">cwicseolfor</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:quicksilver.html>quicksilver</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">living silver</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (see <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">argentum vivum</i>) from its ability to move. See <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">quick</i> in the sense of "living". Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">quick</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">silver</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kwikzilver.html>kwikzilver</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">German Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds-de">Quicksülver</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Quecksilber</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">kviksølv</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bokm%C3%A5l" class="extiw" title="w:Bokmål">Norwegian Bokmål</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nb">kvikksølv</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">kvicksilver</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:quicksilver.html>quicksilver</a></strong> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>The metal mercury.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An amalgam of mercury and tin applied to the <a href = vnd.unilang:backs.html>backs</a> of mirrors, quicksilvering.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">the metal mercury</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">mercury</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">hydrargyrum</span></li></ul>

***quince.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:quince.html>quince</a> (36748)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:quince.html>quince</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">coince</i>, a variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">coins</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">coin</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:quince.html>quince</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">cooing</i> (modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">coing</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cotōneum</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mālum cotōneum</i>, a variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mālum Cydonium</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Cydonian apple</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, translating <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μηλοκυδώνιον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mēlokudṓnion</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:quince.html>quince</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">quinces</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>The pear-shaped fruit of a small tree of the <a href = vnd.unilang:rose.html>rose</a> family, <i>Cydonia oblonga</i>.</li>
<li>The deciduous tree bearing such fruit, native to Asia.</li>
<li>A soft yellow colour, like that of a <a href = vnd.unilang:quince.html>quince</a>.
<dl><dd><div class="color-panel"><a href = vnd.unilang:quince.html>quince</a> colour: <span style="background-color:ECD378; display:inline-block; width:80px;"> </span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">Japan <a href = vnd.unilang:quince.html>quince</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:quince.html>quince</a> curculio</span></li></ul>
</body>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:raadselachtig.html>raadselachtig</a> (32369)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:raadsel.html>raadsel</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-achtig</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:raadselachtig.html>raadselachtig</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:raadselachtig.html>raadselachtiger</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">raadselachtigst</b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:raadsman.html>raadsman</a> (6940)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">raetsman</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:raad.html>raad</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-s-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:raadsman.html>raadsman</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:raadsman.html>raadsmannen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:raadsman.html>raadsmannetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:raadsvrouw.html>raadsvrouw</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> male lawyer, male legal counsel</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The gender-neutral plural <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">raadslieden</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> also commonly used as a plural.

***raaf.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:raaf.html>raaf</a> (16343)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">rāve</i>, formed by reanalysis of the older singular form <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">rāven</i> which <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> reinterpreted as a plural. From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ravan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hrabnaz</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱorh₂-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:raaf.html>raaf</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">raven</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:raaf.html>raafje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A raven, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:corvus.html>Corvus</a> corax</i>.</li>
<li>A raven, term used for certain other large <a href = vnd.unilang:birds.html>birds</a> of the genus <i><a href = vnd.unilang:corvus.html>Corvus</a></i>.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">hoornraaf</span></li></ul>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:raaf.html>raaf</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>

***raam.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:raam.html>raam</a> (1038)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:ramen.html>rame</a></i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">rāme</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh"><a href = vnd.unilang:rama.html>rama</a></i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Rahmen</i>). Origin uncertain, but perhaps related with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">rim</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saterland_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Saterland Frisian">Saterland Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="stq">Rim</i>.
</p>

***raapzaadolie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:raapzaadolie.html>raapzaadolie</a> (80181)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">raapzaad</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:olie.html>olie</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:raapzaadolie.html>raapzaadolie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:raapzaadolie.html>raapzaadoliën</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>oil from the seed of <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Brassica_rapa_subsp._oleifera" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Brassica rapa subsp. oleifera"><i>Brassica <a href = vnd.unilang:rapa.html>rapa</a></i> subsp. <i>oleifera</i></a></span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">raapolie</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Despite the similarity in name, Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:raapzaadolie.html>raapzaadolie</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">raapolie</i> do not refer to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">rapeseed oil</i> but to a closely related oil from field mustard; <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">koolzaadolie</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the Dutch name for what <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> commonly known in English as <i>rapeseed oil</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:raapzaadolie.html>raapzaadolie</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span> / <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span> <sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:voeding.html>voeding</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:plantaardig.html>plantaardige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:olie.html>olie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> koudgeperst <a href = vnd.unilang:wordt.html>wordt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zaden.html>zaden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> raapzaad (<i>Brassica <a href = vnd.unilang:rapa.html>rapa</a></i>) <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verwarren.html>verwarren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> koolzaadolie</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synoniemen"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:synoniemen.html>Synoniemen</a></i></span></h5>
<ul><li>raapolie</li></ul>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
</body> 
***raar.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:raar.html>raar</a> (905)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">raer</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a>, unusual</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (itself rarely occurring), borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">rārus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a>, uncommon</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">raro</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:raar.html>raar</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:raarder.html>raarder</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:raarst.html>raarst</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>strange, odd, weird, unusual</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:raar.html>raar</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:palindroom.html>palindroom</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:vreemd.html>vreemd</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:afwijkend.html>afwijkend</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gewoonlijk.html>gewoonlijk</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:verbazing.html>verbazing</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:opwekkend.html>opwekkend</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>Je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ziet.html>ziet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:soms.html>soms</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:raarste.html>raarste</a></b> niet-bestaande 'Engelse' <a href = vnd.unilang:woorden.html>woorden</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:zoals.html>zoals</a> 'puppydumpen', in Nederlandse <a href = vnd.unilang:kranten.html>kranten</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:racisme.html>racisme</a></i>. ***rad.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:rad.html>rad</a> (13542)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:rat.html>rat</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*rath</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*raþą</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*Hret-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rad.html>rad</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:raderen.html>raderen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:raadje.html>raadje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:radertje.html>radertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl">radje</b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>wheel

***raden.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:raden.html>raden</a> (2128)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">râden</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">rādan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*rēdaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:raden.html>raden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to guess
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">He! <a href = vnd.unilang:weet.html>Weet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a>? <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:spelen.html>spelen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:spel.html>spel</a>! <a href = vnd.unilang:dus.html>Dus</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:luister.html>luister</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vertel.html>vertel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jou.html>jou</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eerste.html>eerste</a> letter <a href = vnd.unilang:zeg.html>zeg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jij.html>jij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mag.html>mag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:raden.html>raden</a></b>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:hey.html>Hey</a>! You know what? <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> [will] play a game! Thus listen good to what I say when I tell you the first letter, and you may <b>guess</b> it [the word]!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to advise</li></ol>
